  <span m="385940">figuring</span> <span m="386460">out</span> <span m="386670">mathematically</span>

  <span m="388830">matching</span> <span m="389300">up</span> <span m="389740">with</span>

  <span m="597050">water</span> <span m="597360">waves,</span> <span m="597790">the</span>
  <span m="597900">property</span> <span m="598320">we're</span> <span m="598450">discussing</span>
  <span m="599150">is</span> <span m="599340">just</span> <span m="599610">the</span>
  <span m="599690">water</span> <span m="600040">level.</span></p><p><span m="601650">So,</span>
  <span m="601990">for</span> <span m="602130">example,</span> <span m="602770">we</span>
  <span m="602870">have</span> <span m="603120">this</span> <span m="603290">average</span>
  <span m="603670">level,</span> <span m="604100">and</span> <span m="604310">then</span>
  <span m="604480">it</span> <span m="604620">can</span> <span m="604780">go</span>
  <span m="604910">high</span> <span m="605240">where</span> <span m="605430">we</span>
  <span m="605550">have</span> <span m="605760">the</span> <span m="605870">peak,</span>
  <span m="606380">or</span> <span m="606690">it</span> <span m="606750">can</span>
  <span m="606910">go</span> <span m="607100">very</span> <span m="607320">low.</span>
  <span m="608160">We</span> <span m="608280">can</span> <span m="608430">also</span>
  <span m="608730">discuss</span> <span m="609310">sound</span> <span m="609660">waves,</span>
  <span m="610010">so</span> <span m="610230">again</span> <span m="610570">it's</span>
  <span m="610720">just</span> <span m="610910">the</span> <span m="610990">periodic</span>
  <span m="611590">variation</span> <span m="612090">of</span> <span m="612200">some</span>
  <span m="612390">property</span> <span m="612656">--</span> <span m="613190">in</span>
  <span m="613390">this</span> <span m="613580">case</span> <span m="613920">we're</span>
  <span m="614060">talking</span> <span m="614460">about</span> <span m="614900">density,</span>
  <span m="615400">so</span> <span m="615550">we</span> <span m="615670">have</span>
  <span m="615890">high</span> <span m="616540">density</span> <span m="616970">areas</span>
  <span m="617460">and</span> <span m="617700">low</span> <span m="617830">density</span>
  <span m="618280">areas.</span></p><p><span m="620730">So,</span> <span m="620930">regardless</span>

  <span m="622310">of</span> <span m="622460">wave</span> <span m="622790">that</span>
  <span m="622930">we're</span> <span m="623040">talking</span> <span m="623460">about,</span>
  <span m="623880">there's</span> <span m="624410">some</span> <span m="624600">common</span>
  <span m="625240">definitions</span> <span m="625920">that</span> <span m="626060">we</span>
  <span m="626140">want</span> <span m="626265">to</span> <span m="626390">make</span>
  <span m="626580">sure</span> <span m="626840">that</span> <span m="627010">we're</span>
  <span m="627130">all</span> <span m="627350">able</span> <span m="627560">to</span>
  <span m="627740">use,</span> <span m="627990">and</span> <span m="628070">the</span>
  <span m="628180">first</span> <span m="628530">is</span> <span m="628710">amplitude.</span>
  <span m="628920">And</span> <span m="628996">when</span> <span m="629072">we're</span>
  <span m="630080">talking</span> <span m="630430">about</span> <span m="630620">the</span>
  <span m="630740">amplitude</span> <span m="631270">of</span> <span m="631370">the</span>
  <span m="631470">wave,</span> <span m="632060">we're</span> <span m="632160">talking</span>
  <span m="632530">about</span> <span m="632750">the</span> <span m="632860">deviation</span>
  <span m="633610">from</span> <span m="633820">that</span> <span m="634060">average</span>
  <span m="634520">level.</span> <span m="635290">So,</span> <span m="635610">if</span>
  <span m="635730">we</span> <span m="635900">define</span> <span m="636490">the</span>

  <span m="637440">zero,</span> <span m="637830">you</span> <span m="637980">can</span>

  <span m="641760">So,</span> <span m="641980">sometimes</span> <span m="642450">people</span>
  <span m="642690">get</span> <span m="642830">confused</span> <span m="643270">when</span>
  <span m="643390">they're</span> <span m="643500">solving</span> <span m="643930">problems</span>

  <span m="644940">amplitude</span> <span m="645480">this</span> <span m="645740">distance</span>

  <span m="648620">but</span> <span m="648860">it's</span> <span m="649010">only</span>
  <span m="649310">half</span> <span m="649650">of</span> <span m="649760">that</span>

  <span m="650490">going</span> <span m="650750">back</span> <span m="650990">to</span>

  <span m="662970">property.</span> <span m="664080">So,</span> <span m="664210">when</span>

  <span m="746450">things,</span> <span m="746780">because</span> <span m="747000">that's</span>

  <span m="749990">electrons.</span></p><p><span m="752780">So,</span> <span m="753470">other</span>

  <span m="774490">on</span> <span m="774610">the</span> <span m="774690">wave,</span>
  <span m="775040">and</span> <span m="775150">it's</span> <span m="775420">the</span>
  <span m="775510">distance</span> <span m="776080">to</span> <span m="776230">that</span>
  <span m="776400">same</span> <span m="776710">point</span> <span m="777840">later</span>

  <span m="780180">one</span> <span m="780460">wavelength.</span> <span m="781580">We</span>
  <span m="781850">also</span> <span m="782250">commonly</span> <span m="782740">discuss</span>
  <span m="783230">the</span> <span m="783320">frequency</span> <span m="784050">of</span>
  <span m="784160">a</span> <span m="784240">wave,</span> <span m="785010">and</span>
  <span m="785230">the</span> <span m="785300">frequency</span> <span m="785800">is</span>

  <span m="787430">that</span> <span m="787630">wave</span> <span m="787950">goes</span>
  <span m="788270">through</span> <span m="788780">per</span> <span m="789080">unit</span>
  <span m="789510">time.</span> <span m="790310">So,</span> <span m="790520">by</span>
  <span m="790673">a</span> <span m="790826">cycle</span> <span m="790980">we'd</span>
  <span m="791370">basically</span> <span m="791950">mean</span> <span m="792420">how</span>
  <span m="792620">many</span> <span m="792820">times</span> <span m="793170">we</span>
  <span m="793290">cycle</span> <span m="793700">through</span> <span m="793980">a</span>
  <span m="794080">complete</span> <span m="794670">wavelength.</span> <span m="795910">So,</span>
  <span m="796230">if</span> <span m="796370">something</span> <span m="796810">cycles</span>
  <span m="797540">through</span> <span m="797860">five</span> <span m="798390">wavelengths</span>
  <span m="799060">in</span> <span m="799180">a</span> <span m="799240">single</span>

  <span m="1028740">of</span> <span m="1029430">2</span> <span m="1029740">pi</span>

  <span m="1033120">And,</span> <span m="1033310">of</span> <span m="1033480">course,</span>
  <span m="1033770">we</span> <span m="1033870">can</span> <span m="1034000">do</span>
  <span m="1034090">the</span> <span m="1034210">same</span> <span m="1034470">thing</span>
  <span m="1034640">again,</span> <span m="1034900">we</span> <span m="1035000">can</span>
  <span m="1035160">think</span> <span m="1035350">about</span> <span m="1035590">when</span>
  <span m="1035770">the</span> <span m="1035920">amplitude</span> <span m="1036240">is</span>
  <span m="1037290">going</span> <span m="1037440">to</span> <span m="1037510">be</span>
  <span m="1037610">at</span> <span m="1037755">its</span> <span m="1037900">maximum,</span>
  <span m="1038710">and</span> <span m="1038860">it's</span> <span m="1039010">going</span>
  <span m="1039135">to</span> <span m="1039260">be</span> <span m="1039770">any</span>
  <span m="1040075">time</span> <span m="1040380">cosine</span> <span m="1041030">of</span>
  <span m="1041190">this</span> <span m="1041350">term</span> <span m="1041700">now</span>
  <span m="1042090">is</span> <span m="1042220">equal</span> <span m="1042550">to</span>
  <span m="1042700">one.</span> <span m="1043490">So</span> <span m="1043605">that</span>
  <span m="1043720">will</span> <span m="1043860">be</span> <span m="1044080">at,</span>
  <span m="1044300">for</span> <span m="1044430">example,</span> <span m="1044930">negative</span>
  <span m="1045390">1</span> <span m="1045630">over</span> <span m="1045860">nu,</span>
  <span m="1046340">or 0,</span> <span m="1046990">or</span> <span m="1047130">1</span>
  <span m="1047350">over</span> <span m="1047570">nu.</span> <span m="1048590">And</span>
  <span m="1048860">again,</span> <span m="1049140">we</span> <span m="1049240">can</span>

  <span m="1051950">we're</span> <span m="1052170">at</span> <span m="1052520">a</span>
  <span m="1052630">maximum.</span></p><p><span m="1055350">So,</span> <span m="1055630">1</span>
  <span m="1056010">over</span> <span m="1056370">nu</span> <span m="1057050">is</span>

  <span m="1058380">use</span> <span m="1058790">and</span> <span m="1058900">we</span>
  <span m="1058990">call</span> <span m="1059250">it</span> <span m="1059340">the</span>

  <span m="1062750">the</span> <span m="1062840">frequency.</span> <span m="1064200">And</span>
  <span m="1064500">if</span> <span m="1064610">we</span> <span m="1064710">think</span>
  <span m="1064910">about</span> <span m="1065180">frequency,</span> <span m="1065670">that's</span>
  <span m="1065910">number</span> <span m="1066300">of</span> <span m="1066450">cycles</span>
  <span m="1067080">per</span> <span m="1067270">unit</span> <span m="1067660">time.</span>
  <span m="1068130">So,</span> <span m="1068390">for</span> <span m="1068500">example,</span>

  <span m="1069610">per</span> <span m="1069760">second,</span> <span m="1070580">whereas</span>
  <span m="1071040">the</span> <span m="1071450">period</span> <span m="1072070">is</span>
  <span m="1072310">how</span> <span m="1072450">much</span> <span m="1072670">time</span>
  <span m="1072940">it</span> <span m="1073030">takes</span> <span m="1073300">for</span>

  <span m="1075000">occur.</span></p><p><span m="1078660">And</span> <span m="1078910">when</span>

  <span m="1081680">case,</span> <span m="1081940">you'll</span> <span m="1082050">be</span>

  <span m="1084470">second.</span> <span m="1085000">So,</span> <span m="1085090">you</span>

  <span m="1217980">the</span> <span m="1218050">wavelength,</span> <span m="1218640">we'll</span>
  <span m="1218780">be</span> <span m="1218910">able</span> <span m="1219080">to</span>
  <span m="1219160">figure</span> <span m="1219430">out</span> <span m="1219560">the</span>
  <span m="1219670">speed.</span> <span m="1220480">But,</span> <span m="1220690">of</span>

  <span m="1221620">very</span> <span m="1221890">special</span> <span m="1222490">about</span>

  <span m="1226320">speed.</span> <span m="1228020">And</span> <span m="1228450">it's</span>
  <span m="1228540">not</span> <span m="1228810">really</span> <span m="1229070">surprising</span>

  <span m="1232770">speed,</span> <span m="1233600">and</span> <span m="1234070">that</span>

  <span m="1236730">and</span> <span m="1237270">typically</span> <span m="1237760">we</span>
  <span m="1237920">abbreviate</span> <span m="1238530">that</span> <span m="1238770">as</span>

  <span m="2103020">that</span> <span m="2103280">light</span> <span m="2103640">constructively</span>
  <span m="2104390">or</span> <span m="2104630">destructively</span> <span m="2106180">could</span>
  <span m="2106350">interfere</span> <span m="2107000">with</span> <span m="2107180">other</span>
  <span m="2107480">light</span> <span m="2108390">waves,</span> <span m="2108800">and</span>
  <span m="2108880">this</span> <span m="2108960">was</span> <span m="2109100">all</span>
  <span m="2109510">confirmed</span> <span m="2111090">and</span> <span m="2111250">visualized.</span>
  <span m="2112300">But</span> <span m="2112900">also,</span> <span m="2113570">around</span>
  <span m="2114740">the</span> <span m="2114860">time</span> <span m="2115320">that</span>
  <span m="2115510">Thomson</span> <span m="2116110">was</span> <span m="2116430">discovering</span>
  <span m="2117010">the</span> <span m="2117080">electron,</span> <span m="2118120">there</span>
  <span m="2118270">were</span> <span m="2118370">some</span> <span m="2118590">other</span>
  <span m="2118790">observations</span> <span m="2119470">that</span> <span m="2119630">were</span>
  <span m="2119710">going</span> <span m="2120070">on,</span> <span m="2120620">and</span>
  <span m="2120830">the</span> <span m="2120890">most</span> <span m="2121170">disturbing</span>
  <span m="2121990">to</span> <span m="2122320">kind</span> <span m="2122660">of</span>
  <span m="2122760">the</span> <span m="2123740">understanding</span> <span m="2124520">of</span>
  <span m="2124630">the</span> <span m="2124730">universe</span> <span m="2125420">was</span>
  <span m="2125610">the</span> <span m="2125730">fact</span> <span m="2126150">that</span>
  <span m="2126290">there</span> <span m="2126410">were</span> <span m="2126500">some</span>
  <span m="2126750">observations</span> <span m="2127520">about</span> <span m="2127820">light</span>

  <span m="2130890">is</span> <span m="2131010">a</span> <span m="2131070">particle.</span>
  <span m="2132600">And</span> <span m="2132760">the</span> <span m="2132840">photoelectric</span>
  <span m="2133090">effect</span> <span m="2133570">is</span> <span m="2134750">maybe</span>
  <span m="2134990">the</span> <span m="2135110">most</span> <span m="2135410">clear</span>
  <span m="2135720">example</span> <span m="2136200">of</span> <span m="2136320">this.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2138440">effect</span> <span m="2139060">is</span> <span m="2139280">the</span>
  <span m="2139390">effect</span> <span m="2139930">that</span> <span m="2140450">if</span>
  <span m="2140630">you</span> <span m="2140750">have</span> <span m="2141180">some</span>

  <span m="2141970">can</span> <span m="2142160">pick</span> <span m="2142400">essentially</span>
  <span m="2142900">any</span> <span m="2143160">metal</span> <span m="2143410">you</span>
  <span m="2143550">want,</span> <span m="2144230">and</span> <span m="2144480">you</span>
  <span m="2144610">shine</span> <span m="2145100">light</span> <span m="2145510">of</span>

  <span m="2146770">onto</span> <span m="2147140">that</span> <span m="2147380">metal,</span>

  <span m="2149290">pop</span> <span m="2149760">off</span> <span m="2150005">an</span>
  <span m="2150250">electron,</span> <span m="2151500">and</span> <span m="2151800">you</span>

  <span m="2152530">and</span> <span m="2152640">measure</span> <span m="2152910">what</span>
